TSAN DGU AA YIG STE BCU YIS MA BCINGS KYANG, DES SDE TSAN GZHAN
RNAMS BCINGS TE,

AAS BCINGS PA'I DBYANGS GSAL PHAN TSUN YANG DAG PAR SBYOR BAR
BYED PAS BSTAN BCOS CHEN PO'I BAR DU 'GRUB PA YIN PA'I PHYIR, DE
'DRA BA'I AA THUNG GANG GIS SHES PA DE NI, MCHOG GI GNAS SAM,
'GRO BA'I BLA MA STE

DRUG DANG, RDO RJE DKYIL 'KHOR

ZHING MAR ME DAG DANG MTSUNGS, ,MI 'GYUR MCHOG TU PHRA BA STE,

KYI RTZA BAR BSTAN

NANG GI MI BSHIG PA'I THIG LE'O, ,DE NI GTZO BO DAM PA YIN TE,
MI 'GYUR BA DANG, SHIN TU PHRA BA DANG, NANG GI DBYANGS GSAL GYI
YIG 'BRU KUN GYI MCHOG

DANG, DON CHEN PO CAN YIN PA'I PHYIR, KHONG NAS 'BYUNG BA SKYE
BA MED, ,CES PA, CHAG GIS, SROG CHEN PO NI YI GE MED, ,CES

KLOG PA DANG NGAG TU

CHAGS BRAL YUL MI 'DOD PA'I RNAM PA CAN CHUNG NGU DANG NI BAR MA
DANG, DE BZHIN DU CHEN PO DAG DANG,

YID LA STE YID PHYIR 'GRO BA DANG, NANG DU 'ONG BA DANG, MYA
NGAN YUL SDUG PA DANG BRAL BA'I SEMS GDUNG CHUNG NGU LA SOGS PA
GSUM DANG, DE BZHIN DU SEMS RNAL DU 'DUG PA'I ZHI BA DANG, RNAM
RTOG RGOD CING SEMS

RTZING BAR RTOG PA DANG, MI SDUG PA DANG PHRAD NA SEMS 'JIGS PA
DANG, 'JIGS PA BAR MA DANG, SHIN TU 'JIGS PA DANG, YUL LA ZHEN
PA'I SRED PA DANG, SRED PA BAR MA DANG, SHIN TU SRED PA DANG,
'DOD PA'I YUL

RNAMS 'DZIN PA'I LEN PA DANG, MI DGE BA LA YID GNYIS ZA BA'AM,
RANG GI SEMS MI GSOD PA DANG, BKRES PA ZAS DANG, SKOM PA BTUNG
BA 'DOD PA 'DI DANG, BDE SDUG BTANG SNYOMS GSUM GYI TSOR BA
DANG,

TSOR BA BAR MA DANG, SHIN TU TSOR BA'I SKAD CIG STE SO SOR PHYE
BA DANG, RIG PA PO DANG, RIG BYA'I LAS DANG, 'DZIN TE, RIG PAR
BYED PA GSUM LA RTOG PA GSUM DANG, 'DIR BZHI ZHES PA RGYA DPE MA
DAG PA'O, ,RIGS

PA DANG MI RIGS PA SO SOR DPYOD PA DANG, RANG NGAM CHOS RGYU
MTSAN DU BYAS NAS KHA NA MA THO BA LA 'DZEM PA'I NGO TSA SHES PA
DANG, SDUG BSNGAL BRAL 'DOD KYI SNYING RJE DANG, DMIGS BYA

@039B NAM MKHA' LTA BU'I SNANG BA YANG MI GA-YO BA BRTAN PAR
GYUR PA STE 'GYUR RO, ,RLUNG SNANG BA DANG PO GNYIS KYI RGYUR
GYUR BAS NI, DE JI LTA BAR BDAG GI DNGOS POR RNAM PAR BRTAGS PA
SNANG BA NYER THOB PA STE, SNGAR LTAR THABS SHES KYI YE

SHES GNYIS 'DRES PA'I GNYIS KA'I YAN LAG NYID DU 'GYUR BA'I
PHYIR RO, ,GNYIS PA STONG PA GSUM GYI YE SHES SKYE TSUL STON PA
LA, ,SGYU MA DAG NI THAMS CAD LAS, ,BUD MED SGYU MA KHYAD PAR
'PHAGS, ,YE SHES GSUM GYI DBYE BA

NI, ,GSAL BAR 'DI LAS MTSON PAR 'GYUR, ,'DOD CHAGS NYID DANG
CHAGS BRAL DANG, ,DE YI BAR TE GSUM PO NI, ,DBANG PO GNYIS NI
MNYAM SBYOR BA'I, ,RDO RJE PADMA 'DUS LAS SO, ,YE SHES GNYIS NI
MNYAM SBYOR BAS, ,

MNYAM PAR SBYOR BAR BSHAD PA YIN, ,YE SHES GNYIS KYI MNYAM SBYOR
DANG, ,JI SKAD BSHAD PA'I BYA BA YIS, ,'BAD PAS YE SHES GANG
THOB PA, ,DE NI SNANG BA THOB PA'O, ,GANG ZHIG CHU SKYES RDO RJE
SBYOR, ,KUN RDZOB TU YANG MED GYUR

NA, ,LAN CIG TZAM ZHIG MYONG NAS KYANG, ,RNAL 'BYOR STOBS KYIS
'GRUB PAR 'GYUR, ,YE SHES 'JUG PA'I NGO BO YIS, ,DBYE BA JI
